/*! HeartBeatTracker - v1.2 - 2019-11-27 */

window.HeartBeatTracker = function() {
    var MediaHeartbeat = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat;
    var MediaHeartbeatConfig = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeatConfig;
    var MediaHeartbeatDelegate = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeatDelegate;

    //  "this object override
    var _this = this;

    //  Players list
    //  Players are keyed on playerId
    this.players = {};


    //  Static configuration parameters set at DTM level
    this.configuration = _satellite.getVar("[VIDEO] HbConfiguration");

    //  AppMeasurement object - set at global level
    this.appMeasurement = window.s;

    //  Create HeartBeat Media Object
    //  Params:
    //      - contextData
    //      - video_data
    //          - video_id
    //          - video_name
    //          - video_length
    //          - video_ovp
    //      - jwPlayerObject

    this.createHBPlayer = function(params) {

        //  Get JWPlayer ID.
        var player_id = params.jwPlayerObject.getConfig().id;
        var player = false;
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: ",
        //    "PlayerID ", player_id);       

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: linkTrackVars: ", s.linkTrackVars);
        s.linkTrackVars = "";
        s.clearVars();

        //    Workaround to convert videoID to String
        if (typeof params.video_data.video_id != "string")
            params.video_data.video_id = params.video_data.video_id.toString();

        // Verifico che non esista un player del video
        if (typeof _this.players[player_id] != "undefined") {
            // _satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: ",
            //     "HBPlayer for --> ",
            //     player_id,
            //     "",
            //     " already exists.");
            player = _this.players[player_id]
        } else {
            //  Create l'istanza della classe VideoHeartBeat Player for the video_id
            player = new HeartBeatPlayer(
                params,
                this.configuration,
                this.appMeasurement
            );

            _this.players[player_id] = player;
            //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:",
            //    "HBPlayer for --> ",
            //  player_id,
            //  "",
            //  " CREATED!");
        }

        //  Controllare che la sessione non sia già iniziata
        //  Inizio la session tracking (quando cambiano i video senza ADV)
        if (!player.isTrackingSessionActive) {
            _trackSessionStart(params, player);
            player.isTrackingSessionActive = true;
        }
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: linkTrackVars: ", s.linkTrackVars);
    }

    //  VIDEO CORE PLAYBACK
    //  Method to track video play
    this.HBTrackPlay = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: player state on track play: " , player.player.getState())

        //  Workaround to convert videoID to String
        if (typeof params.video_data.video_id != "string")
            params.video_data.video_id = params.video_data.video_id.toString();


        //  Check to avoid double playTracking
        if (player.isTracking)
            return false;

        //  Controllare che la sessione non sia già iniziata
        //  Inizio la session tracking (quando cambiano i video senza ADV)
        /*if (!player.isTrackingSessionActive) {
            _trackSessionStart(params, player);
            player.isTrackingSessionActive = true;
        }*/

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackPlay();

        //  Check to avoid double playTracking
        player.isTracking = true;
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: ",
        //  "HBPlayer -->", params.player_id, "--> PLAYSTART ")
        // _satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: Video ",
        //     params.video_data.video_name);
    }

    //  Method to track video complete
    this.HBTrackPause = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackPause();

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //   " HBPlayer --> " +
        //  params.player_id + " TRACK PAUSE called.");
    }

    //  Method to track video complete
    this.HBTrackComplete = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackComplete();

        player.isTracking = false;
        
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:",
        //  " HBPlayer --> ",
        //  params.player_id, " TRACK COMPLETE and SESSION END called.");
    }

    //  Method to stop the session when the video is unloaded, without completing
    this.destroyHBPlayer = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackSessionEnd();

        player.isTracking = false;
        player.isTrackingSessionActive = false;

        delete _this.players[params.player_id];

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:",
        //  " HBPlayer --> ",
        //  params.player_id, "SESSION END without TRACK COMPLETE called.");
    }

    //  END VIDEO CORE PLAYBACK

    //  AD TRACKING

    //  Method to track AdBreakStart
    //  params:
    //  - player_id
    //  - ad_break_params
    //      - ad_break_name: "preroll",
    //      - position: 0,
    //      - start_time: 0

    this.HBTrackAdBreakStart = function(params) {
        // console.log("---- Track Ad Break Start 1")

        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        var _adBreakInfo = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.createAdBreakObject(
            params.ad_break_params.ad_break_name,
            params.ad_break_params.position,
            params.ad_break_params.start_time);

        // console.log("---- Track Ad Break Start 2")



        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdBreakStart, _adBreakInfo, null);

        // console.log("---- Track Ad Break Start 3")

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //   " HBPlayer --> " +
        //  " --> TRACK AD BREAK START called.");
    }

    //  Method to track AdStart
    //  params:
    //  - player_id
    //  - ad_params
    //      - ad_name
    //      - ad_id
    //      - position
    //      - length

    this.HBTrackAdStart = function(params) {

        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];


        var _adObject = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.createAdObject(
            params.ad_params.ad_name,
            params.ad_params.ad_id,
            params.ad_params.position,
            params.ad_params.length);

        //AD name -> The name of the ad 
        //AD id -> The unique id for the ad
        //AD position -> The start position of the ad (number)
        //AD length -> The length of the ad in second (number)

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdStart, _adObject, null);

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //  " HBPlayer --> " +
        //  params.player_id +
        //  " --> AdTitle: " +
        //  params.ad_params.ad_name +
        //  " --> TRACK AD START called.");
    }

    this.HBTrackAdSkip = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: player state before skip: " + player.player.getState())
        //  [31.01.2019] Rimosso momentaneamente per il live.   
        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdSkip);

        // _satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER: player state after skip: " + player.player.getState())
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //  " HBPlayer --> " +
        //  params.player_id + " TRACK AD SKIP called.");
    }

    this.HBTrackAdComplete = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        //  [31.01.2019] Rimosso momentaneamente per il live.
        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdComplete);
        //player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdBreakComplete);

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //   " HBPlayer --> " +
        //  params.player_id + " TRACK AD COMPLETE called.");
    }

    this.HBTrackAdBreakEnd = function(params) {
        var player = _this.players[params.player_id];

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdBreakComplete);

        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER:" +
        //  " HBPlayer --> " + " TRACK AD BREAK END called.");
    }

    //  END AD TRACKING


    //  INTERNAL METHOD
    var _trackSessionStart = function(params, player) {
        //_satellite.notify("---- HEARTBEATTRACKER --> _trackSessionStart");

        var mediaObject = undefined;
        var customVideoMetadata = params.contextData;

        mediaObject = MediaHeartbeat.createMediaObject(params.video_data.video_name,
            params.video_data.video_id,
            params.video_data.video_length,
            params.video_data.video_ovp);

        player.my_mediaHeartbeat.trackSessionStart(mediaObject, customVideoMetadata);
    }
}


//  Class to manage MediaObjectInstances
var HeartBeatPlayer = function(params, Configuration, _appMeasurement) {

    var MediaHeartbeat = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeat;
    var MediaHeartbeatConfig = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeatConfig;
    var MediaHeartbeatDelegate = ADB.va.MediaHeartbeatDelegate;

    var _this = this;
    this.video_params = params;
    this.player = params.jwPlayerObject;

    // Config
    this.mediaConfig = new MediaHeartbeatConfig();
    this.mediaConfig.trackingServer = Configuration.HEARTBEAT.TRACKING_SERVER;
    this.mediaConfig.playerName = Configuration.PLAYER.NAME;
    this.mediaConfig.channel = Configuration.HEARTBEAT.CHANNEL;
    this.mediaConfig.debugLogging = false;
    this.mediaConfig.appVersion = Configuration.HEARTBEAT.SDK;
    this.mediaConfig.ssl = true;
    this.mediaConfig.ovp = Configuration.HEARTBEAT.OVP;

    // Delegate
    this.mediaDelegate = new MediaHeartbeatDelegate();

    // Replace <currentPlaybackTime> with the video player current playback time
    this.mediaDelegate.getCurrentPlaybackTime = function() {
        return _this.player.getCurrentTime();
    };

    this.mediaDelegate.getQoSObject = function() {
        return MediaHeartbeat.createQoSObject(5000, 0, 24, 10);
    };

    this.my_mediaHeartbeat =
        new MediaHeartbeat(this.mediaDelegate, this.mediaConfig, _appMeasurement);
}

// Il codice JavaScript a seguire verifica puntualmente l'accettazione del
// consenso Sky Data Service, scatenando opportuni eventi in gestione al
// Datalake.
if (typeof __tcfapi === 'function') {
  var idSkyDataService = '6109863b5c1e7805bd9e652f';

  // Gestione registrazione funzione di callback della CMP per "catturare" live
  // o in pageview eventuali interazioni con la gestione dei consensi.
  __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function(tcData) {
    if(tcData.eventStatus == 'useractioncomplete') {
      // Verifica puntuale consensi Sky Data Service
      __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents) {
        var skyDataServiceConsent = false;

        if (vendorConsents && vendorConsents.consentedVendors) {
          for(var i = 0, size = vendorConsents.consentedVendors.length; i < size; ++i) {
            if(vendorConsents.consentedVendors[i]._id == idSkyDataService) {
              skyDataServiceConsent = 'true';
              break;
            }
          }
        }

        if(skyDataServiceConsent) {
          console.info('CMP - Sky Data Service accettato');

          s.linkTrackVars = 'events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = s.events = 'event200';
          s.tl(this, 'o', 'click_cmp_accetta');
        }
        else {
          console.info('CMP - Sky Data Service NON accettato');

          s.linkTrackVars = 'events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = s.events = 'event199';
          s.tl(this, 'o', 'click_cmp_rifiuta');
        }
      });
    }
  });
}
else {
  console.error("CMP API not available");
}
});</script></body>
